                "Send Message - Payment": {
                  "summary": "",
                  "description": "\n<p>\n    <strong>MESSAGE_BODY</strong>: The body of the payment item. There’s a maximum of 1024 characters. <br />\n    <strong>MESSAGE_BODY_SIZE</strong>: The character length of the parts-&gt;data. <br />\n    <strong>MESSAGE_HEADER</strong>: The header data of the payment item. Text for the header. Maximum of 60 characters <br />\n    <strong>MESSAGE_FOOTER</strong>: The footer data of the payment item. There’s a maximum of 60 characters. <br />\n    <strong>REFERENCE_ID</strong>: <strong>Required.</strong> Unique identifier for the order or invoice provided by the business. This cannot be an empty string and can only contain English letters, numbers, underscores, dashes, or dots,\n    and should not exceed 35 characters. The reference_id must be unique for each order_details message for a given business. If there is a need to send multiple order_details messages for the same order, it is recommended to include a\n    sequence number in the reference_id (for example, “BM345A-12”) to ensure reference_id uniqueness.<br />\n    <strong>TYPE</strong>: <strong>Required.</strong> Must be one of “digital-goods” or “physical-goods” <br />\n    <strong>beneficiaries</strong>: <strong>Required for shipped physical-goods.</strong> An array of beneficiaries for this order. A beneficiary is an intended recipient for the delivery of <strong>physical goods</strong> in the order.\n    <br />\n    <strong>BENEFICIARY_NAME</strong>: <strong>Required.</strong> Name of the individual or business receiving the physical goods. Cannot exceed 200 characters <br />\n    <strong>BENEFICIARY_ADDRESS_LINE1</strong>: <strong>Required.</strong> Shipping address (Door/Tower Number, Street Name etc.).
